In [11]:
# address: split long list of data into different columns
df['address_list'] = df['address'].str.split(',')
df['street'] = df['address_list'].apply(lambda col: col[0])
df['city'] = df['address_list'].apply(lambda col: col[1])
df['zipcode'] = df['address_list'].apply(lambda col: col[2])
df['country'] = df['address_list'].apply(lambda col: col[3])

In [16]:
# Create seperate columns for sqft_living and sqft_lot
df['area.sqft_living/sqft_lot_list1'] = df['area.sqft_living/sqft_lot_list'].apply(lambda col: col[1])

df['area.sqft_lot'] = df['area.sqft_living/sqft_lot_list2'].apply(lambda col: col[1])
